\Anax\TextFilter

\Anax\TextFilterTextFilter

Extract frontmatter from text and pass text through a set of filter to format and extract information from the text.

addRevisionHistory()

addRevisionHistory(string  $text, array  $revision, string  $start, string  $end, string  $class, string  $source = null) : string

with content.
